<td style="text-align:right;padding:0;vertical-align:middle;width:45%"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/Bundesautobahn_4" title="Bundesautobahn 4">A 4</a></span> <img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c5/Bundesautobahn_4_number.svg/34px-Bundesautobahn_4_number.svg.png" width="34" height="20" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c5/Bundesautobahn_4_number.svg/50px-Bundesautobahn_4_number.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c5/Bundesautobahn_4_number.svg/67px-Bundesautobahn_4_number.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="400" data-file-height="240" /> →</td>

<p><b>Bundesautobahn&#160;3</b> (translates from <a href="/wiki/German_language" title="German language">German</a> as <i>Federal Motorway&#160;3</i>, short form <b>Autobahn&#160;3</b>, abbreviated as <b>BAB&#160;3</b> or <b>A&#160;3</b>) is an <a href="/wiki/Autobahn" title="Autobahn">autobahn</a> in <a href="/wiki/Germany" title="Germany">Germany</a> that links the border with the <a href="/wiki/Netherlands" title="Netherlands">Netherlands</a> near <a href="/wiki/Wesel" title="Wesel">Wesel</a> in the northwest to then go to the A2/A516 in Oberhausen then go's to the south at the <a href="/wiki/Austria" title="Austria">Austrian</a> border near <a href="/wiki/Passau" title="Passau">Passau</a> as then being the <a href="/wiki/Innkreis_Autobahn" title="Innkreis Autobahn">A8</a>.</p>
<p>Major cities along its total length of 778&#160;km (483&#160;mi) include <a href="/wiki/Oberhausen" title="Oberhausen">Oberhausen</a>, <a href="/wiki/Duisburg" title="Duisburg">Duisburg</a>, <a href="/wiki/D%C3%BCsseldorf" title="Düsseldorf">Düsseldorf</a>, <a href="/wiki/Leverkusen" title="Leverkusen">Leverkusen</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cologne" title="Cologne">Cologne</a>, <a href="/wiki/Wiesbaden" title="Wiesbaden">Wiesbaden</a>, <a href="/wiki/Frankfurt" title="Frankfurt">Frankfurt</a>, <a href="/wiki/W%C3%BCrzburg" title="Würzburg">Würzburg</a>, <a href="/wiki/Nuremberg" title="Nuremberg">Nuremberg</a> and <a href="/wiki/Regensburg" title="Regensburg">Regensburg</a>. The A&#160;3 is a major connection between the <a href="/wiki/Rhine-Ruhr" title="Rhine-Ruhr">Rhine-Ruhr</a> area and southern Germany, resulting in heavy traffic. Consequently, large parts have three lanes (plus emergency lane) in each direction, including a 300&#160;km (187.5&#160;mi) long part between Oberhausen and <a href="/wiki/Aschaffenburg" title="Aschaffenburg">Aschaffenburg</a>.</p>
<p></p>

<h2>Contents</h2>
</div>

<p></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="History">History</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Bundesautobahn_3&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: History">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<table class="plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-content ambox-Refimprove" role="presentation">
<tr>
<td class="mbox-image">
<div style="width:52px"><a href="/wiki/File:Question_book-new.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/50px-Question_book-new.svg.png" width="50" height="39" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/75px-Question_book-new.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/100px-Question_book-new.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="512" data-file-height="399" /></a></div>
</td>
<td class="mbox-text"><span class="mbox-text-span">This section <b>needs additional citations for <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">verification</a></b>. <span class="hide-when-compact">Please help <a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Bundesautobahn_3&amp;action=edit">improve this article</a> by <a href="/wiki/Help:Introduction_to_referencing_with_Wiki_Markup/1" title="Help:Introduction to referencing with Wiki Markup/1">adding citations to reliable sources</a>. Unsourced material may be challenged and removed.</span> <small><i>(February 2008)</i></small> <small class="hide-when-compact"><i>(<a href="/wiki/Help:Maintenance_template_removal" title="Help:Maintenance template removal">Learn how and when to remove this template message</a>)</i></small></span></td>
</tr>
</table>
<div class="thumb tleft">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Bundesarchiv_B_145_Bild-F088783-0003,_Bei_Bad_Honnef,_Ferienverkehr_auf_der_A_3.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/08/Bundesarchiv_B_145_Bild-F088783-0003%2C_Bei_Bad_Honnef%2C_Ferienverkehr_auf_der_A_3.jpg/220px-Bundesarchiv_B_145_Bild-F088783-0003%2C_Bei_Bad_Honnef%2C_Ferienverkehr_auf_der_A_3.jpg" width="220" height="144" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/08/Bundesarchiv_B_145_Bild-F088783-0003%2C_Bei_Bad_Honnef%2C_Ferienverkehr_auf_der_A_3.jpg/330px-Bundesarchiv_B_145_Bild-F088783-0003%2C_Bei_Bad_Honnef%2C_Ferienverkehr_auf_der_A_3.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/08/Bundesarchiv_B_145_Bild-F088783-0003%2C_Bei_Bad_Honnef%2C_Ferienverkehr_auf_der_A_3.jpg/440px-Bundesarchiv_B_145_Bild-F088783-0003%2C_Bei_Bad_Honnef%2C_Ferienverkehr_auf_der_A_3.jpg 2x" data-file-width="800" data-file-height="524" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Bundesarchiv_B_145_Bild-F088783-0003,_Bei_Bad_Honnef,_Ferienverkehr_auf_der_A_3.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
The A3 in 1991</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The first plans for the segment between Cologne and Düsseldorf date to 1925, and a bypass segment 2.5 kilometres (1.6&#160;mi) long at <a href="/wiki/Opladen" title="Opladen">Opladen</a> was built beginning in 1931 and opened on 27 September 1933. The remainder of the highway between <a href="/wiki/Oberhausen" title="Oberhausen">Oberhausen</a> and Wiesbaden via Cologne was constructed in sections as part of the <a href="/wiki/Reichsautobahn" title="Reichsautobahn">Reichsautobahn</a> network, until 1940. The first of these, the 25 kilometres (16&#160;mi) segment between Cologne-Mülheim and Hilden, opened on 21 May 1936. The 41.5 kilometres (25.8&#160;mi) stretch between Limburg and Dierdorf opened on 15 June 1940, and that between Erlangen and Nuremberg was completed in 1941, although in one direction only over part of the segment. However, work on the stretch south of Wiesbaden, including the bridge over the <a href="/wiki/Main_(river)" title="Main (river)">Main</a> at Eddersheim, was suspended in 1943. The northern segment to the border with the Netherlands, the so-called "Holland Line", was begun in 1939 and suspended in 1942; work resumed on this segment in 1958 and it opened in sections between 1961 and 1965. Work also began in 1939 on a segment between <a href="/wiki/Regensburg" title="Regensburg">Regensburg</a> and <a href="/wiki/W%C3%B6rth_an_der_Donau" title="Wörth an der Donau">Wörth an der Donau</a>, which was to have included a bridge over the <a href="/wiki/Danube" title="Danube">Danube</a> at Regensburg and a bypass north of <a href="/wiki/Deggendorf" title="Deggendorf">Deggendorf</a>, but work was suspended in or before 1942, and this segment (passing south of Deggendorf instead of north) was only completed in the 1960s. The parts in Eastern <a href="/wiki/Bavaria" title="Bavaria">Bavaria</a> were built significantly later, with the last gaps being closed in 1984.</p>
<p>The A&#160;3 runs parallel to the <a href="/wiki/Bundesstra%C3%9Fe_8" title="Bundesstraße 8">Bundesstraße 8</a>, which it thus replaced as a main highway. Both follow the medieval trade route <i>Via Publica</i> that was first mentioned in a document from 839.</p>
<div style="clear:left;"></div>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Current_state">Current state</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Bundesautobahn_3&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Current state">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:BAB3_Koelner_Ring.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/eb/BAB3_Koelner_Ring.jpg/220px-BAB3_Koelner_Ring.jpg" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/eb/BAB3_Koelner_Ring.jpg/330px-BAB3_Koelner_Ring.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/eb/BAB3_Koelner_Ring.jpg/440px-BAB3_Koelner_Ring.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1600" data-file-height="1200" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:BAB3_Koelner_Ring.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
the <a href="/wiki/Cologne_Beltway" title="Cologne Beltway">Cologne Beltway</a></div>
</div>
</div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Netherlands_to_Cologne">Netherlands to Cologne</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Bundesautobahn_3&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Netherlands to Cologne">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The A3 is four-laning for the first 65 kilometers (41&#160;mi) up from the Dutch border. There are six lanes, three lanes in each direction, between interchange <i>Kreuz Oberhausen</i> and <i>Köln-Mülheim</i>. On a short part inside of <i>Kreuz Kaiserberg</i> the A3 has two lanes. The Autobahn is equipped with eight lanes on the <a href="/wiki/Cologne_Beltway" title="Cologne Beltway">Cologne Beltway</a> between <i>Köln-Mülheim</i> and autobahn triangle <i>Dreieck Köln-Heumar</i>.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Cologne_to_Aschaffenburg">Cologne to Aschaffenburg</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Bundesautobahn_3&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Cologne to Aschaffenburg">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The course until Waldaschaff near <a href="/wiki/Aschaffenburg" title="Aschaffenburg">Aschaffenburg</a> has six lanes. The A3 is seven-laning between <i>Mönchhofer Dreieck</i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Wiesbadener_Kreuz" title="Wiesbadener Kreuz">Wiesbadener Kreuz</a></i> (four lanes in the direction of Cologne, three to Würzburg) and eight-laning between <i>Frankfurter Kreuz</i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Offenbacher_Kreuz" title="Offenbacher Kreuz">Offenbacher Kreuz</a></i>.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Aschaffenburg_to_F.C3.BCrth">Aschaffenburg to Fürth</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Bundesautobahn_3&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Aschaffenburg to Fürth">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The A3 has only four lanes from <i>Aschaffenburg-Ost</i> to the junction with the A&#160;73 <i>Kreuz Fürth/Erlangen</i> in year 2009. The <i>Spessart</i>-slope near Waldaschaff and some slope areas near Würzburg have additional lanes. There are plans to expand this area of the A3 up to six lanes in the next few years. The construction between <i>Hösbach</i> and <i>Bessenbach/Waldaschaff</i> was finished in 2011, and the new building of the <i>Haseltalbrücke</i> was terminated in 2012. The section in the area of Würzburg — from the border between <a href="/wiki/Baden-W%C3%BCrttemberg" title="Baden-Württemberg">Baden-Württemberg</a> and <a href="/wiki/Bavaria" title="Bavaria">Bavaria</a> near <i>Helmstadt</i> to <i>Würzburg-Heidingsfeld</i> and from <i>Würzburg/Rottendorf</i> to <i>Rottendorf</i> — was expanded until 2012. The next kilometers between <i>Rottendorf</i> and interchange <i>Kreuz Biebelried</i> will be finished in late 2012. It is planned to start the expansion of the last section near Würzburg — between <i>Würzburg-Heidingsfeld</i> and <i>Würzburg/Rottendorf</i> — in 2013.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="F.C3.BCrth_to_Austria">Fürth to Austria</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Bundesautobahn_3&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Fürth to Austria">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>There are six lanes between <i>Kreuz Fürth/Erlangen</i> and <i>Kreuz Nürnberg</i> while the remaining section towards the Austrian border only has two lanes in each direction.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Special">Special</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Bundesautobahn_3&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Special">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Between Cologne and Frankfurt an <a href="/wiki/Intercity-Express" title="Intercity-Express">ICE</a> high-speed railway line (300&#160;km/h) closely follows the A&#160;3's route.</p>
<p>Two sections in the Frankfurt area are equipped with a special kind of facility to allow a temporary release of the emergency lanes during the rush hour. The section between <i>Hanau</i> and <i>Offenbacher Kreuz</i> and also the section between <i>Kelsterbach</i> and <i>Mönchhofdreieck</i> have this facility, so that a further lane for each direction can be opened. These sections are monitored by cameras, so that the additional lane can be closed in critical situations, for example in case of a vehicle breakdown.</p>
<p>Some parts of the A3 are among the most busy roads in Germany. According to a survey from 2010, three sections are in the Top 10 of roads with major average traffic each day. Only the Berlin city autobahn <a href="/wiki/Bundesautobahn_100" title="Bundesautobahn 100">A100</a> had more traffic in 2010.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup></p>
<ul>
<li>5th place: <i>Kreuz <a href="/wiki/Leverkusen" title="Leverkusen">Leverkusen</a> – Leverkusen</i> = 157.600 vehicles</li>
<li>6th place: <i><a href="/wiki/K%C3%B6ln" class="mw-redirect" title="Köln">Köln</a>-Dellbrück – Kreuz Köln-Ost</i> = 157.100 vehicles</li>
<li>8th place: <i><a href="/wiki/Frankfurt" title="Frankfurt">Frankfurt</a>-Süd – <a href="/wiki/Offenbach_am_Main" title="Offenbach am Main">Offenbacher</a> Kreuz</i> = 150.700 vehicles</li>
</ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Plans_and_construction">Plans and construction</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Bundesautobahn_3&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Plans and construction">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul>
<li>An upgrade to eight lanes is planned with urgent demand between Leverkusen and Cologne</li>
<li>An upgrade to eight lanes is planned with urgent demand near Frankfurt</li>
<li>The upgrade to six lanes from Aschaffenburg to Schlüsselfeld is also planned with urgent demand
<ul>
<li>The section between <i>Rottendorf</i> and <i>Kreuz Biebelried</i> (4,0&#160;km / 2,5&#160;mi) is under construction since 2009 to late 2012.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The upgrade to six lanes from <i>Schlüsselfeld</i> to <i>Kreuz Fürth/Erlangen</i> is planned with further demand</li>
<li>An upgrade to six lanes near Regensburg is planned with urgent demand</li>
</ul>
